Having started his career in renowned clubs such as the Paradise Garage and Studio 54, the New York City resident is widely considered as one of the forefathers of house music.  Kevorkian now tours the world, taking part in many music gatherings, such as the Midem (France), Sónar Festival of Advanced Music and Multimedia Art (Spain), Global Gathering (UK), Exit Festival (Serbia), The Big Chill (UK), Bestival (UK) and Electric Picnic (Ireland).\n\nFrançois K Boiler Room\nPlays: 139,738\n\n\n\n\nDJ SPINN \nFacebook  Twitter  Soundcloud\nTEKLIFE FOUNDER / FOOTWORK PIONEER / PRODUCER / DJ / MC  Coming up from nothing to something is a hell of an accomplishment, that's why when it comes to DJ SPINN that feat is highly attainable. Whether writing, dj'ing, dancing or producing SPINN always stayed on top of his game. So by 1998, SPINN had a following that loved the style of house tracks he and long time buddy DJ RASHAD were creating - this style later developed into what is todays juke movement.\n\nDJ Spinn - Full Set - Pitchfork Music Festival 2014\nPlays: 589,298\n\n\n\n\nDJ TAYE \nFacebook  Twitter  Soundcloud\nChicago footwork producer DJ Taye made his name as one of the youngest artists affiliated with the Teklife crew, which he joined in 2010. Born in 1994, he began making hip-hop beats and rapping at age 11, and was introduced to the sounds of DJ Rashad and DJ Spinn in 2007. Entranced by the head-spinning beats, booming bass, and frantically cut-up samples, he began producing his own tracks in that style, and eventually racked up several digital releases and mix sessions. Tracks by Taye appeared on Hyperdub's 2014 compilations Hyperdub 10.1 and Next Life, and the label signed him, releasing his debut vinyl EP, Break It Down, the following year.\n\nDJ Taye - Burnin Ya Boa feat DJ Manny\nPlays: 17,172\n\n\n\n\nJAY DANIEL \nFacebook  Twitter  Soundcloud\nLots of young producers claim not to give a fuck, but act like they do.
